***уха.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>уха</a> (18820)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>уха</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uxa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*juxa</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*yew(ǝ)-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to blend, mix (food), knead</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ius</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">यूष</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">yūṣa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>уха́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uxá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уха.html>ухи́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>ukha, a Russian fish soup</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́ха</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">úxa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">genitive singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́хо</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">úxo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table class="morfotable ru" style="float:right; clear:right; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse; max-width:300px;" cellpadding="3" rules="all">

***ухаживать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухаживать.html>уха́живать</a> (5802)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уходить.html>уходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uxodítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to care for, to look after</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, <span class="ann-pos">perfective</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухаживать.html>уха́живать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uxáživatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to care, to tend, to nurse, to look after
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>Весь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:месяц.html>ме́сяц</a> а́нна <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ухаживать.html>уха́живала</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свое́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сестра.html>сестро́й</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vesʹ mésjac Ánna <b>uxáživala</b> za svojéj bolʹnój sestrój.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Anna <b>looked after</b> her sick sister for a whole month.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to court, to date</li></ol>

***ухать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухать.html>у́хать</a> (16597)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухать.html>у́хать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">úxatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухнуть.html>у́хнуть</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***ухватиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухватиться.html>ухвати́ться</a> (5714)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухватить.html>ухвати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uxvatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухватиться.html>ухвати́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uxvatítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ухва́тываться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to catch/lay hold <i>(of)</i>, to grasp
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ухватиться.html>ухвати́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перила.html>пери́ла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uxvatítʹsja</b> za períla</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to grip/grasp/seize the (hand)rail</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to snatch <i>(at)</i>, to grasp <i>(at)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ухватиться.html>ухвати́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случай.html>слу́чай</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uxvatítʹsja</b> za slúčaj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to seize an opportunity</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ухватиться.html>ухвати́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мысль</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uxvatítʹsja</b> za predložénije (za myslʹ)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to jump at an offer (at the idea)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ухватиться.html>ухвати́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>uxvatílsja</b> za éto predložénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he snatched at (grasped at) the offer</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухватить.html>ухвати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uxvatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хитрить.html>хитри́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xitrítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухмыляться.html>ухмыля́вшийся</a> (8709)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Per Vasmer, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">smollen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to smile</span><span annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to smile</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, archaic <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">smuylen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to smile</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bavarian_language" class="extiw" <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">smolla</i> <span <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухнуть.html>у́хнуть</a> (13332)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухнуть.html>у́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">úxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухать.html>у́хать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to crash, to bang
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">где́-то <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ухнуть.html>у́хнул</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:снаряд.html>снаря́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gdé-to <b>úxnul</b> snarjád</i> ― <span class="e-translation">somewhere a shell exploded with a crash</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to hoot</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to squander, to lose at one stroke</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slip, to fall
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ухнуть.html>у́хнула</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́му</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mašína <b>úxnula</b> v jámu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the car dived into a pit</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to bang, to slap
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ухнуть.html>у́хнуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кулак.html>кулако́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>столу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>úxnutʹ</b> kulakóm po stolú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bang one's fist on the table</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ух.html>ух</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ux</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уханье.html>у́ханье</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uxanʹje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***ухо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́хо</a> (395)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*uxo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂ṓws</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classical_Armenian" class="extiw" title="w:Classical Armenian">Old Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" lang="xcl">ունկն</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xcl-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">unkn</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌰𐌿𐍃𐍉</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ausō</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">οὖς</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oûs</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">auris</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">هوش</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hūš, hōš</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">intellect</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́хо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">úxo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́ха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́ши</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>уше́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикладывать.html>прикла́дывать</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:приложить.html>приложи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́ху</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prikládyvatʹ/priložítʹ časý k <b>úxu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put a watch to one's ear</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уходить.html>уходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uxodítʹ</span>, <span class="ann-pos">perfective</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уход.html>ухо́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uxód</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уход.html>ухо́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уход.html>ухо́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уход.html>ухо́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>care <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">treatment of those in need</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:уход.html>ухо́д</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больны́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пожилой.html>пожило́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:возраст.html>во́зраста</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дому́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uxód</b> za bolʹnými požilóvo vózrasta na domú</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>care</b> for the sick elderlies at home</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уходить.html>уходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uxodítʹ</span>, <span class="ann-pos">imperfective</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уход.html>ухо́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uxód</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уход.html>ухо́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уход.html>ухо́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уход.html>ухо́дов</a></b>)

***уходить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уходить.html>уходи́ть</a> (396)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уходить.html>уходи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uxodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уйти.html>уйти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to leave, to depart, to go (away) (by foot)</li>
<li>to escape, to evade</li>
<li>to resign, to retire</li>
<li>to be lost</li>
<li>to fail</li>
<li>to sink, to plunge</li>
<li>to be spent</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уходить.html>уходи́ть</a></span></b> is a Russian abstract verb. Its counterpart, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уйти.html>уйти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ujtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, is a concrete verb.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уходить.html>уходи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uxodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">folk  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to exhaust, to torment</li>
<li>to look after, to care for (someone) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually only used in the past passive participle</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<table style="float:right; clear:right; padding:3; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" class="morfotable ru">

***ухудшавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухудшать.html>ухудша́вший</a> (29332)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухудшать.html>ухудша́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uxudšávšij</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухудшение.html>ухудше́ние</a> (9774)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухудшить.html>уху́дшить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uxúdšitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухудшение.html>ухудше́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uxudšénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухудшение.html>ухудше́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухудшение.html>ухудше́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухудшение.html>ухудше́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>worsening, deterioration</li></ol>
